Key RPC Methods and Their Purpose\n\n### Pod Sandbox Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `RunPodSandbox` | Creates and starts a pod-level sandbox (network namespace, cgroups) |\n| `StopPodSandbox` | Stops sandbox processes and reclaims network resources |\n| `RemovePodSandbox` | Removes the sandbox completely |\n| `PodSandboxStatus` | Returns status including IP addresses, state |\n| `ListPodSandbox` | Lists all sandboxes with optional filtering |\n| `PodSandboxStats` | Returns resource usage metrics for a sandbox |\n| `UpdatePodSandboxResources` | Updates cgroup resource constraints |\n| `PortForward` | Sets up port forwarding to a sandbox |\n\n### Container Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `CreateContainer` | Creates a container in a specified pod sandbox |\n| `StartContainer` | Starts a created container |\n| `StopContainer` | Stops a running container with grace period |\n| `RemoveContainer` | Removes a container |\n| `ListContainers` | Lists containers with filtering |\n| `ContainerStatus` | Returns container state, exit code, timestamps |\n| `UpdateContainerResources` | Updates container cgroup limits |\n| `ReopenContainerLog` | Reopens stdout/stderr log files |\n\n### Exec/Streaming Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `ExecSync` | Runs command synchronously, returns output |\n| `Exec` | Prepares streaming endpoint for command execution |\n| `Attach` | Attaches to running container's stdin/stdout/stderr |\n\n### Image Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `ListImages` | Lists all images |\n| `ImageStatus` | Returns image details (size, digests) |\n| `PullImage` | Pulls image with authentication |\n| `RemoveImage` | Removes an image |\n| `ImageFsInfo` | Returns filesystem usage for images |\n\n## 3. Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Plugin Registration\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/plugins/cri/cri.go`\n\nContainerd registers its CRI implementation as a gRPC plugin:\n\n```go\nfunc init() {\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,\n            plugins.EventPlugin,\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,\n        },\n        InitFn: initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n```\n\nThe plugin imports the CRI proto types directly from Kubernetes:\n```go\nimport runtime \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\"\n```\n\n### Core Service Implementation\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe `criService` struct implements both `RuntimeServiceServer` and `ImageServiceServer`:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    config             criconfig.Config\n    sandboxStore       *sandboxstore.Store\n    containerStore     *containerstore.Store\n    sandboxNameIndex   *registrar.Registrar\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n    netPlugin          map[string]cni.CNI\n    client             *containerd.Client\n    streamServer       streaming.Server\n    eventMonitor       *events.EventMonitor\n    // ... additional fields\n}\n```\n\n### CRI Method Implementations\n\nEach CRI RPC method is implemented in a dedicated file:\n\n| CRI Method | Implementation File | Line |\n|------------|---------------------|------|\n| `RunPodSandbox` | `sandbox_run.go` | 53 |\n| `StopPodSandbox` | `sandbox_stop.go` | - Generate unique ID and reserve sandbox name\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n    c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id)\n\n    // 2. Create lease for resource management\n    ls, _ := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n\n    // 3. Get OCI runtime configuration\n    ociRuntime, _ := c.config.GetSandboxRuntime(config, r.GetRuntimeHandler())\n\n    // 4. Create sandbox metadata\n    sandbox := sandboxstore.NewSandbox(...)\n\n    // 5. Setup network namespace (if not host network)\n    if !hostNetwork(config) {\n        sandbox.NetNS, _ = netns.NewNetNS(netnsMountDir)\n        c.setupPodNetwork(ctx, &sandbox)\n    }\n\n    // 6. Create and start sandbox via sandbox controller\n    c.sandboxService.CreateSandbox(ctx, sandboxInfo, ...)\n    ctrl, _ := c.sandboxService.StartSandbox(ctx, sandbox.Sandboxer, id)\n\n    // 7. Return sandbox ID\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{PodSandboxId: id}, nil\n}\n```\n\n### Example: CreateContainer Implementation\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/container_create.go:60`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) CreateContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.CreateContainerRequest) (_ *runtime.CreateContainerResponse, retErr error) {\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n    sandboxConfig := r.GetSandboxConfig()\n    sandbox, _ := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n\n    // 1. Generate container ID and reserve name\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    name := makeContainerName(metadata, sandboxConfig.GetMetadata())\n\n    // 2. Build OCI runtime spec (platform-specific)\n    spec, _ := c.buildContainerSpec(...)  // calls buildLinuxSpec, buildWindowsSpec, etc.\n\n    // 3. Create container in containerd\n    container, _ := c.client.NewContainer(ctx, id, containerOpts...)\n\n    // 4. Store container metadata\n    c.containerStore.Add(containerstore.Container{...})\n\n    return &runtime.CreateContainerResponse{ContainerId: id}, nil\n}\n```\n\n## 4. 6. Key Implementation Details\n\n### Idempotent Operations\nStop and Remove operations are idempotent - they don't return errors if resources are already in the desired state. This is required by the CRI specification.\n\n### Name Uniqueness\nBoth sandbox and container names are tracked via `registrar.Registrar` to ensure uniqueness across the namespace.\n\n### Platform Support\ncontainerd provides platform-specific implementations:\n- `container_create_linux.go`\n- `container_create_windows.go`\n- `container_create_other.go`\n\n### Resource Management\nLeases are used to track resource lifecycle, ensuring cleanup even on failures.\n\n### Instrumentation\nThe `instrument` package wraps all CRI calls for metrics and tracing:\n```go\nfunc (c *Old_criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n## Summary\n\nThe CRI interface provides a clean contract between Kubernetes and container runtimes:\n\n1. **Kubernetes** defines the CRI proto at `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n2. **containerd** implements the CRI as a plugin at `plugins/cri/cri.go`\n3. The actual method implementations live in `internal/cri/server/*.go`\n4. **Kubernetes vendors** containerd's low-level API types for direct containerd communication when needed\n5. Both gRPC and ttrpc protocols are supported for kubelet-to-containerd communication\n",

RuntimeConfig(RuntimeConfigRequest) returns (RuntimeConfigResponse) {}\n\n    // UpdatePodSandboxResources updates pod sandbox resources constraints.\n    rpc UpdatePodSandboxResources(UpdatePodSandboxResourcesRequest) returns (UpdatePodSandboxResourcesResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n### ImageService Definition (lines 143-166)\n\n```protobuf\nservice ImageService {\n    // ListImages lists existing images.\n    rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageStatus returns the status of the image.\n    rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n    rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveImage removes the image.\n    rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n    rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n## 2. Key RPC Methods and Their Purpose\n\n### Pod Sandbox Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `RunPodSandbox` | Creates and starts a pod-level sandbox (network namespace, cgroups) |\n| `StopPodSandbox` | Stops sandbox processes and reclaims network resources |\n| `RemovePodSandbox` | Removes the sandbox completely |\n| `PodSandboxStatus` | Returns status including IP addresses, state |\n| `ListPodSandbox` | Lists all sandboxes with optional filtering |\n| `PodSandboxStats` | Returns resource usage metrics for a sandbox |\n| `UpdatePodSandboxResources` | Updates cgroup resource constraints |\n| `PortForward` | Sets up port forwarding to a sandbox |\n\n### Container Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `CreateContainer` | Creates a container in a specified pod sandbox |\n| `StartContainer` | Starts a created container |\n| `StopContainer` | Stops a running container with grace period |\n| `RemoveContainer` | Removes a container |\n| `ListContainers` | Lists containers with filtering |\n| `ContainerStatus` | Returns container state, exit code, timestamps |\n| `UpdateContainerResources` | Updates container cgroup limits |\n| `ReopenContainerLog` | Reopens stdout/stderr log files |\n\n### Exec/Streaming Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `ExecSync` | Runs command synchronously, returns output |\n| `Exec` | Prepares streaming endpoint for command execution |\n| `Attach` | Attaches to running container's stdin/stdout/stderr |\n\n### Image Operations\n\n| RPC Method | Purpose |\n|------------|---------|\n| `ListImages` | Lists all images |\n| `ImageStatus` | Returns image details (size, digests) |\n| `PullImage` | Pulls image with authentication |\n| `RemoveImage` | Removes an image |\n| `ImageFsInfo` | Returns filesystem usage for images |\n\n## 3. Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Plugin Registration\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/plugins/cri/cri.go`\n\nContainerd registers its CRI implementation as a gRPC plugin:\n\n```go\nfunc init() {\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,\n            plugins.EventPlugin,\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,\n        },\n        InitFn: initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n```\n\nThe plugin imports the CRI proto types directly from Kubernetes:\n```go\nimport runtime \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\"\n```\n\n### Core Service Implementation\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe `criService` struct implements both `RuntimeServiceServer` and `ImageServiceServer`:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    config             criconfig.Config\n    sandboxStore       *sandboxstore.Store\n    containerStore     *containerstore.Store\n    sandboxNameIndex   *registrar.Registrar\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n    netPlugin          map[string]cni.CNI\n    client             *containerd.Client\n    streamServer       streaming.Server\n    eventMonitor       *events.EventMonitor\n    // ... additional fields\n}\n```\n\n### CRI Method Implementations\n\nEach CRI RPC method is implemented in a dedicated file:\n\n| CRI Method | Implementation File | Line |\n|------------|---------------------|------|\n| `RunPodSandbox` | `sandbox_run.go` | 53 |\n| `StopPodSandbox` | `sandbox_stop.go` | - |\n| `RemovePodSandbox` | `sandbox_remove.go` | - |\n| `PodSandboxStatus` | `sandbox_status.go` | - |\n| `ListPodSandbox` | `sandbox_list.go` | - |\n| `CreateContainer` | `container_create.go` | 60 |\n| `StartContainer` | `container_start.go` | 45 |\n| `StopContainer` | `container_stop.go` | 39 |\n| `RemoveContainer` | `container_remove.go` | 34 |\n| `ListContainers` | `container_list.go` | - |\n| `ContainerStatus` | `container_status.go` | - |\n| `ExecSync` | `container_execsync.go` | - |\n| `Exec` | `container_exec.go` | - |\n| `Attach` | `container_attach.go` | - |\n\n### Example: RunPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go:53`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (_ *runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, retErr error) {\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and reserve sandbox name\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n    c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id)\n\n    // 2. Create lease for resource management\n    ls, _ := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n\n    // 3. Get OCI runtime configuration\n    ociRuntime, _ := c.config.GetSandboxRuntime(config, r.GetRuntimeHandler())\n\n    // 4. Create sandbox metadata\n    sandbox := sandboxstore.NewSandbox(...)\n\n    // 5. Setup network namespace (if not host network)\n    if !hostNetwork(config) {\n        sandbox.NetNS, _ = netns.NewNetNS(netnsMountDir)\n        c.setupPodNetwork(ctx, &sandbox)\n    }\n\n    // 6. Create and start sandbox via sandbox controller\n    c.sandboxService.CreateSandbox(ctx, sandboxInfo, ...)\n    ctrl, _ := c.sandboxService.StartSandbox(ctx, sandbox.Sandboxer, id)\n\n    // 7. Return sandbox ID\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{PodSandboxId: id}, nil\n}\n```\n\n### Example: CreateContainer Implementation\n\n**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/container_create.go:60`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) CreateContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.CreateContainerRequest) (_ *runtime.CreateContainerResponse, retErr error) {\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n    sandboxConfig := r.GetSandboxConfig()\n    sandbox, _ := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n\n    // 1. Generate container ID and reserve name\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    name := makeContainerName(metadata, sandboxConfig.GetMetadata())\n\n    // 2. Build OCI runtime spec (platform-specific)\n    spec, _ := c.buildContainerSpec(...)  // calls buildLinuxSpec, buildWindowsSpec, etc.\n\n    // 3. Create container in containerd\n    container, _ := c.client.NewContainer(ctx, id, containerOpts...)\n\n    // 4. Store container metadata\n    c.containerStore.Add(containerstore.Container{...})\n\n    return &runtime.CreateContainerResponse{ContainerId: id}, nil\n}\n```\n\n## 4. 6. Key Implementation Details\n\n### Idempotent Operations\nStop and Remove operations are idempotent - they don't return errors if resources are already in the desired state. This is required by the CRI specification.\n\n### Name Uniqueness\nBoth sandbox and container names are tracked via `registrar.Registrar` to ensure uniqueness across the namespace.\n\n### Platform Support\ncontainerd provides platform-specific implementations:\n- `container_create_linux.go`\n- `container_create_windows.go`\n- `container_create_other.go`\n\n### Resource Management\nLeases are used to track resource lifecycle, ensuring cleanup even on failures.\n\n### Instrumentation\nThe `instrument` package wraps all CRI calls for metrics and tracing:\n```go\nfunc (c *Old_criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n## Summary\n\nThe CRI interface provides a clean contract between Kubernetes and container runtimes:\n\n1. **Kubernetes** defines the CRI proto at `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n2. **containerd** implements the CRI as a plugin at `plugins/cri/cri.go`\n3. The actual method implementations live in `internal/cri/server/*.go`\n4. **Kubernetes vendors** containerd's low-level API types for direct containerd communication when needed\n5. Both gRPC and ttrpc protocols are supported for kubelet-to-containerd communication\n",

# Tracing Kubernetes CRI from gRPC Definition to containerd Implementation

This document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition in the kubernetes repository to containerd's implementation of those interfaces.

## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition

**Location:** `/ccb_crossrepo/src/kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`

The CRI defines two primary gRPC services:
- `RuntimeService` - Manages containers and pod sandboxes
- `ImageService` - Manages container images

### RuntimeService Definition (lines 24-140)

```protobuf
service RuntimeService {
    // Version returns the runtime name, runtime version, and runtime API version.
    rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse) {}

    // RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes must ensure
    // the sandbox is in the ready state on success.
    rpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}

    // StopPodSandbox stops any running process that is part of the sandbox and
    // reclaims network resources (e.g., IP addresses) allocated to the sandbox.
    rpc StopPodSandbox(StopPodSandboxRequest) returns (StopPodSandboxResponse) {}

    // RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox.
    rpc RemovePodSandbox(RemovePodSandboxRequest) returns (RemovePodSandboxResponse) {}

    // PodSandboxStatus returns the status of the PodSandbox.
    rpc PodSandboxStatus(PodSandboxStatusRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatusResponse) {}

    // ListPodSandbox returns a list of PodSandboxes.
    rpc ListPodSandbox(ListPodSandboxRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxResponse) {}

    // CreateContainer creates a new container in specified PodSandbox
    rpc CreateContainer(CreateContainerRequest) returns (CreateCont
... (truncated)
